< text>
Jeff Jenkins is a wonderful chiropractor and an extraordinary man. I have been a client of his for over six years since moving up from Southern California to the Bay Area in 2009. During that time, he has provided me with chiropractic and message therapy care on a once per monthly basis (on average).

"Dr. J," as affectionately referred to by his patients, has always been immensely energetic, extremely caring, and devoted to my care. I have observed the same treatment from him on patients coming in before and after me, without fail. What I love about Dr. J is that he actually spends quality time with me; he listens to my condition, responds with preventive care recommendations, and best of all, provides a thorough hand and machine-assisted body massage prior to performing a series of expert adjustments at key areas on my neck, back, hips and shoulders.

He has a wealth of Chiropractic experience, bolstered by a specialty in message therapy, which he leverages generously in treating his patients. I have been to other DCs in the past, and they provide much less time and attention, focusing only on adjustments and never incorporating any massage therapy or table traction work.

Lastly and perhaps most importantly; Dr. J is a motivational force; he effectively lives a life of personal accountability and positivity, and encourages his patients to do the same. His personal anecdotes and empowering stories provide a steady source "rich mental protein" for those of us who ride the treadmill of corporate work-life existence. He dishes them out generously while graciously doing his work for you on the traction table.

"Your Life. Your Responsibility" is a mainstay of encouragement at the office, and it shows in the atmosphere there; you can literally feel it from his patients and their families. It's wonderful to have an example of such a nurturing and caring doctor in the face of a changing healthcare system that puts increasing pressure on healthcare providers like Dr. J by controlling and limiting service reimbursement.

I recommend Dr. J to anyone looking for chronic or recurring pain relief (due to repetitive stress or otherwise), and especially those who wish to stay physically active well into their 30s and 40s. I credit my ability to run and swim regularly and pain-free to his routine care. I also recommend Dr. J as a generous and compassionate healthcare provider.<//text>

I explained to Priscila the details of what happened that night. I explained to her that it was not my first time at this location and that Usually the staff is Very Helpful and Friendly. However, that night this was not the case. I told her that upon placing my order at the drive-thru I asked the person taking the order to Please Not place ice in the drink. I had been experiencing flu-like symptoms and I thought the ice Would worsen this. When I arrived to the window to pay, the young lady by the name of "Teresa" (I know this b/c that was the name on the receipt) handed the drink to me. I Immediately noticed it had ice and Politely told her that I had asked for the drink with No Ice. What she stated next not only shocked me but it Extremely upset me as well. She stated "Well you should have told me when you placed the order!" Her manner was like she was scolding Me and she actually seemed upset for those couple of seconds.
I then stated to her that I Did let her know that I asked for No Ice in the drink. At No point did this young lady even take the time to apologize for a simple mistake. THAT to me was Even More upsetting! So I asked her for her name, to which she RUDELY replied "It's On The Receipt!" I then asked if her manager was available, to which she replied "I Am the manager." I asked her if she could please give me the name and number of her district manager and she again, stated yet Even More upset, "You can look it up online!"
I was Extremely Shocked and UPSET so I decided to place the formal complaint on the company's website. The JITB representative (Priscila) listened to what I had to say and the details of my experience that night. She Formally Apologized and Genuinely Understood and Empathized with my concerns. She Definitely "made-up" for the Extremely bad experience I had gone through that night. I would Definitely recommend this location to friends and family however, if something doesn't seem right then let it be known. And if you do "formally" complain for any reason rest assured that your issue Will Be addressed by JITB!<//text>

I recently bought a used vehicle, which failed the smog test on visual, functional, and emissions. The smog tech at Joe's took time to advise me on what to look out for, what to fix and return for the free retest. I followed his advice, and found additional malfunctioning parts that I replaced on my own with some online research. <Text>I must say this is one of the smallest, non descript pot shops I have ever been too. The place looked crowded just with the two guys and a girl behind the counter, the three employees that were working.
On first entering the store and taking quick note of the sparse looking inventory in the small display counter second thoughts about buying anything from this place ran through my mind.
But then one of the guys almost immediately offered a sample joint for my friend and I to smoke and long story short my friend and I left with our purchases, both of us high as a kite and completely satisfied with the experience. The product we bought turned out to be of high quality, no pun intended, but it fits. And the counter dude who acted as the main salesman was full of personality, being helpful and suggestive selling without being obnoxious about it, and he was hot to boot. Not a large variety of product there, but top quality for sure. I  recommend it.<//Text>< Pictures>

<rate>3<//rate>< Review>
I was looking for a place that would be able to trim my hair in layers.

Jessica's Hair & Nail Salon was the closest in the area, and I made an appointment. They were able to squeeze me in on the same day that I called.  While I arrived on time, once I opened the door, I saw the "CASH ONLY" sign and panicked. I had no cash on me.  I asked if I could run to the bank and come back.  They were fine with it.  Unfortunately, my bank was 3 miles away and it was prime traffic time. I didn't come back with the cash until 40-50 minutes later. They still took me in for the haircut fortunately.

Once I sat on the chair, a female staff member prepped my hair. Mid-way through she for some reason couldn't continue, so one of the male staff ended up cutting my hair.  I appreciated his patience and precision. What I didn't appreciate was the remarks made in Vietnamese by the woman, not knowing that I'm Vietnamese too!  I felt like she was a distraction to the guy cutting my hair, and I really could not relax at all.

The haircut was priced around $35, and I left a nice tip for the person cutting my hair.  While the hair cut was decent, I didn't enjoy the overall experience.  This place is CASH ONLY so be prepared.

For now, I'll still continue to search for a hairdresser I can trust with my locks!<//Review>

< Review>
So I was somewhat disappointed with the service I received today.  When I decided to use Solar Maintenance Pros for my panel cleaning I was told the service technicians would take before and after photos of the roof and panels (I was concerned about tile breakage during the service) and would check connections, wiring, inverter, etc.  The service kinda went like this; two technicians arrived at the house, went on the roof, one sprayed the panels the other used a brush.  When they were done one of the technicians knocked on my door and handed me an invoice.  As he walked away I asked about my roof tiles , if any were broke during the service.  He responded there were several cracked tiles to which I responded was odd because about 40 tiles were changed during the solar installation less than a year ago.  I expected for him to offer to show me before and after photos but he never offered.  Also, while I did not expect any issues, I was never told the system looked okay which one would expect if an inspection was a part of the service.  The bottom line is they came out cleaned the panels and left.  If a company claims to do specific things then the client should be advised of the observations, and I would have liked to see the before and after photos of my roof and panels.  Now I have to climb on the roof to look myself.  On a positive note the technicians did showed up on time and gave me a heads up phone call and from what I can see from the ground the panels look much better than before the service.<//Review>

I finally decided to get solar and knew I wanted a local company to do the installation.  I spent months researching and finally decided to go with Solar Negotiators (Now Solar Maintenance Pros), as they were local, had great reviews, and the owner was a Veteran, being a Veteran myself this played a big role.  I'll leave names out just to keep things as objective as possible.

I met with my sales representative and planned out my system.  I was paying cash as I didn't want to hassle with yet another loan.  As everyone who goes solar knows, it's a big investment and something that isn't taken lightly.  From this point, I was thoroughly satisfied with the process.

My project got turned over to the service team and I was assigned a service representative to oversee my project and be my point of contact from here on out.  This was February 22, 2019.  From here I was given the checklist and approximate timelines.

The Site Survey went off without any problems.  The plans were submitted and I signed off on it.  A few days later I was told there were problems with my plans and they sent over a second draft for my approval.  I signed the second draft and awaited install day.

Install day came and when I got home I noticed the panels were in the wrong area.  Long story short, the original plans were given to the installers, not the newest approved plans.  After a little back and forth, I think they did a great job on resolving this issue.  Instead of moving the rack, they just added a new rack and gave me 2 free panels to offset the shade issue and as a way to make up for the confusion on their end.

My system went from 4.7kW to 5.2kW.  Therefore it had to go back to the city for approval, which delayed the process.  I'm 62 days into my project; I have panels on my roof, an inverter on my wall, a brand new electrical panel and I'm still getting all my electricity from PG&E.  I'm just waiting to find out what the next step is, I've reached out and haven't got any communication back.

So all this to say the following:  I wish Solar Maintenance Pros did a better job with communication.  Maybe not everyday, but send an email at least every other day with a status, even if it's just "still waiting on the city to approve your project".  I worked in the service industry and I called my customer's everyday to let them know what was going on with their computer, they appreciated the constant communication.  It reassured them and let them know that their computer/project was important.  People want to know what's going on, especially with a project that costs so much.  This is a huge investment, I am by no means wealthy, so this took me a long time to save up for.  I don't like being left out in the dark.</Review>

< Review>
This was a long researched project for us. We spent over 2 years researching & interviewing multiple solar installers. The price ranges from Sunrun, Tesla, etc were huge. Some were twice the price of Solar Negotiators!!

Our project was unique but not impossible and we needed some special things done for optimal production of our ground mount solar panels.

Again and again when we found the panels we wanted, the installation was too expensive. Then when we found an affordable installer he wanted use cheap solar panels or had bad reviews or wasn't local.

So here is how we made our decision.
Ask these questions:

How are their reviews on google, yelp, etc?
Are they a local company?
Are they knowledgeable on solar?
Do they come out and inspect the install site or use google earth?
How many installations have they done?
How often do they clean the panels?
What kind of warranty do they provide for loss production on the panels?

Happy to say Solar Negotiators checked all the boxes. We could not be happier with our experience with the install and customer service. They love what they do and it shows in their work and attention to detail.

I would highly recommend them to any of my closest friends.

**Remember that 2019 is the last year of the full 30% Fed Rebate**.

Scott H
O'Neals, Ca</Review>
